      <h2> Find a driver test appointment </h2> 

      <p>Our dedicated driver testing centre at St Marys has bookings available. When you <a data-entity-substitution="canonical" data-entity-type="linky" data-entity-uuid="25e18b98-8e55-4eba-bf9f-591e8b23b69a" href="https://www.myrta.com/wps/poc/extvp?uri=urlresolver%3Atbsloginredirect&WASReqURL=/wps/mypoc/extvp%3Furi%3Durlresolver%3Atbsinit&tranCode=tbs">book online</a>, select St Marys as a location to find available dates and times. </p>

          <h3 id="quiet-hour-is-available-in-selected-service-centres">Quiet Hour is available in selected service centres</h3> 

          <p>Selected service centres in Sydney and regional areas are trialling <a data-entity-substitution="canonical" data-entity-type="linky" data-entity-uuid="1ddb7a94-b094-462c-a505-b2d459480edf" href="/about-us/our-organisation/supporting-customers-with-disability" data-ga4-link-type="link_internal">Quiet Hour.</a></p> 

         </div>
